    598  35e8							;----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    599  35e8							; handle pause button for 2600 and 7800
    600  35e8
    601  35e8							; Timings:  NOT including palette setting or platform detect
    602  35e8							; 2600:     no button press:	 11 cycles
    603  35e8							;	     with button press:  21 cycles
    604  35e8							; 7800      no button press:	 16 cycles
    605  35e8							;	     with button press:  21 cycles
    606  35e8
    607  35e8
    608  35e8
    609  35e8		       00 08	   BW_SWITCH  =	$08	; NOTE: Shares bit position with SWCHB COLOUR/B&W SWITCH
    610  35e8
    611  35e8		       24 80		      bit	gameMode
    612  35ea		       50 0b		      bvc	.pause7800	; 7800 platform
    613  35ec
    614  35ec							; 2600 pause logic...
    615  35ec
    616  35ec		       ad 82 02 	      lda	SWCHB
    617  35ef		       45 80		      eor	gameMode
    618  35f1		       29 08		      and	#BW_SWITCH
    619  35f3		       f0 17		      beq	.setPauseCol	; no different to original state = no pause change
    620  35f5		       d0 0f		      bne	.buttonDown	; unconditional
    621  35f7
    622  35f7							; 7800 pause logic...
    623  35f7
    624  35f7							; When the button is pressed, we check if it's the FIRST time it's pressed.
    625  35f7							; This FIRST time is indicated by the PFLAG7800 being clear.  If it's the first time, we toggle the pause
    626  35f7							; flag (BIT6) AND we toggle the PFLAG7800 so continued button-down does nothing.  When the button is
    627  35f7							; released, then we again toggle the PFLAG7800, allowing a FIRST time check once again, when the button
    628  35f7							; is next pressed.
    629  35f7
    630  35f7		       a9 08	   .pause7800 lda	#BW_SWITCH
    631  35f9		       2c 82 02 	      bit	SWCHB
    632  35fc		       f0 04		      beq	.pausePress
    633  35fe		       05 80		      ora	gameMode	; not pressed, so enable first time press
    634  3600		       d0 08		      bne	.fixPause	; unconditional
    635  3602
    636  3602		       24 80	   .pausePress bit	gameMode
    637  3604		       f0 06		      beq	.setPauseCol	; NOT the first time in pause - so do nothing new
    638  3606
    639  3606							; Button is down, and we have detected it as a FIRST-TIME button press.
    640  3606
    641  3606		       45 80	   .buttonDown eor	gameMode	; toggle first time flag(7800) or current switch state(2600)
    642  3608		       49 80		      eor	#GAMEMODE_PAUSED	; toggle pause flag
    643  360a		       85 80	   .fixPause  sta	gameMode
    644  360c
    645  360c		       a5 80	   .setPauseCol lda	gameMode	; are we paused?
    646  360e		       10 07		      bpl	.exitPause	; only show pause colour when actually paused
    647  3610
    648  3610		       a6 81		      ldx	Platform
    649  3612		       bd 83 f6 	      lda	pscol,x
    650  3615		       85 af		      sta	BGColour	; set main screen background colour.  RED is paused.
    651  3617
    652  3617				   .exitPause
    653  3617

    655  3617
    656  3617							; has to be done AFTER screen display, because it disables the effect!

    658  3619		       85 62		      sta	HMM0	; 3	 this assumes that HMOVE is called at least once/frame

    673  362b
    674  362b							; Handle the player joystick reading. We do it *every frame* so that we can incorporate a two-frame
    675  362b							; buffer.  This is designed to give a little better responsiveness to the 'quick tap' movement.
    676  362b
    677  362b		       a5 95		      lda	BufferedJoystick	; previous frame
    678  362d		       85 96		      sta	BufferedJoystick+1	; -> buffered
    679  362f
    680  362f							; Create a 'standardised' joystick with D4-D7 having bits CLEAR if the appropriate direction is chosen.
    681  362f							; P2 is shifted UP, so we don't need to worry in usage elsewhere (it's same format as a P1 joystick)
    682  362f
    683  362f		       a5 9e		      lda	whichPlayer	; 3
    684  3631		       25 ac		      and	jtoggle	; 3
    685  3633		       aa		      tax		; 2

    688  3636		       85 97		      sta	BufferedButton	; 3 = 15

    696  363f		       0a		      asl		; 2
    697  3640		       0a		      asl		; 2

    699  3642		       85 95	   notP2      sta	BufferedJoystick	; 3

    714  3652
    715  3652							;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    716  3652							; Player animation happens *every* frame so that we get good animation speeds.  Note that
    717  3652							; the player animation consists of running a small animation 'program', and then actually drawing
    718  3652							; the player.	The draw is the neat bit, because all it does is update some self-modifying pointers
    719  3652							; inside the actual draw kernel in the appropriate bank.
    720  3652
    721  3652
      0  3652					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	AnimatePlayers	; in GENERIC_BANK_1
      1  3652		       00 06	   BANK_AnimatePlayers =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  3652					      SUBROUTINE
      3  3652				   AnimatePlayers
    723  3652
    724  3652							; Optimised 7/1/2012 -- single page tables
    725  3652
    726  3652							; This interesting code performs the animations for the player(s) and sets the
    727  3652							; pointers INSIDE the row bank for the draw code to point to the correct player
    728  3652							; shape.  Kind of neat, as it doesn't require any shape copying (=speed!)
    729  3652
    730  3652
    731  3652							; Cycle the player through his animation list.  The animation of a player is a direct
    732  3652							; pointer to the actual shape used to display the player.  This shape is in turn
    733  3652							; written to the current bank's self-modifying locations for the draw.  Since
    734  3652							; we are effectively drawing from this current bank, the same code can be used
    735  3652							; to 'undraw' the player as required.
    736  3652
    737  3652
    738  3652							; x = player index
    739  3652							; sets ManAnimation = FRAME to display for player
    740  3652							; ManAnimation = index of player program into Manimate list
    741  3652
    742  3652		       24 80		      bit	gameMode
    743  3654		       30 2c		      bmi	AnimationOK	; don't animate during pause
    744  3656
    745  3656		       c6 a4		      dec	ManDelayCount
    746  3658		       10 28		      bpl	AnimationOK
    747  365a
    748  365a		       a4 a5	   ReloadAnimation ldy	ManAnimation
    749  365c		       b9 00 f5    ContinueAnim lda	Manimate,y	; delay count
    750  365f		       d0 07		      bne	NewFrameOK
    751  3661		       b9 01 f5 	      lda	Manimate+1,y
    752  3664		       a8		      tay
    753  3665		       4c 5c f6 	      jmp	ContinueAnim
    754  3668
    755  3668		       10 0d	   NewFrameOK bpl	doDelay
    756  366a
    757  366a		       c8		      iny		; handle a REFLECT
    758  366b		       a5 a8		      lda	ManLastDirection
    759  366d		       29 f7		      and	#%11110111
    760  366f		       19 00 f5 	      ora	Manimate,y
    761  3672		       85 a8		      sta	ManLastDirection
    762  3674
    763  3674		       c8		      iny
    764  3675		       d0 e5		      bne	ContinueAnim
    765  3677
    766  3677		       85 a4	   doDelay    sta	ManDelayCount
    767  3679
    768  3679		       c8		      iny
    769  367a		       b9 00 f5 	      lda	Manimate,y
    770  367d		       85 a7		      sta	ManAnimationFrameLO
    771  367f
    772  367f		       c8		      iny
    773  3680		       84 a5		      sty	ManAnimation
    774  3682
    775  3682		       60	   AnimationOK rts
    776  3683

------- FILE i2c_v2.2.inc LEVEL 3 PASS 3
      0  3687					      include	"i2c_v2.2.inc"
      1  3687							;
      2  3687							; i2c_v2.2.inc
      3  3687							;
      4  3687							;
      5  3687							; AtariVox EEPROM Driver
      6  3687							;
      7  3687							; By Alex Herbert, 2004
      8  3687							;
      9  3687							; Optimisations by Thomas Jentzsch, 2006/2008
     10  3687							;
     11  3687
     12  3687
     13  3687							; I/O Constants
     14  3687
     15  3687		       00 04	   I2C_SDA_MASK equ	$04
     16  3687		       00 08	   I2C_SCL_MASK equ	$08
     17  3687
     18  3687
     19  3687							; Signalling Macros
     20  3687
     21  3687							;  MAC     I2C_SCL_0
     22  3687							;    lda     #$00
     23  3687							;    sta     SWCHA
     24  3687							;  ENDM
     25  3687
     26  3687							;  MAC     I2C_SCL_1
     27  3687							;    lda     #I2C_SCL_MASK
     28  3687							;    sta     SWCHA
     29  3687							;  ENDM
     30  3687
     31  3687							;  MAC     I2C_SDA_IN
     32  3687							;    lda     #I2C_SCL_MASK
     33  3687							;    sta     SWACNT
     34  3687							;  ENDM
     35  3687
     36  3687							;  MAC     I2C_SDA_OUT
     37  3687							;    lda     #I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK
     38  3687							;    sta     SWACNT
     39  3687							;  ENDM
     40  3687
     41  3687
     42  3687					      MAC	i2c_start
     43  3687							; I2C_SCL_1
     44  3687					      lda	#(I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK)*2	; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK
     45  3687					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
     46  3687							; I2C_SDA_OUT
     47  3687					      lsr		; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK
     48  3687					      sta	SWACNT	; 4
     49  3687							; total: 12 cycles
     50  3687					      ENDM
     51  3687
     52  3687
     53  3687					      MAC	i2c_txbit
     54  3687							; I2C_SCL_0
     55  3687					      lda	#%0011	; 2
     56  3687					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
     57  3687							; set bit
     58  3687					      adc	#%1000	; 2
     59  3687					      sta	SWACNT	; 4	     SDA = !C (a = %1000 / %1100)
     60  3687							; I2C_SCL_1
     61  3687					      lda	#I2C_SCL_MASK	; 2
     62  3687					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
     63  3687							; total: 18 cycles
     64  3687					      ENDM
     65  3687
     66  3687
     67  3687					      MAC	i2c_txnack
     68  3687							; I2C_SCL_0
     69  3687					      lda	#I2C_SCL_MASK*2	; 2	     $00
     70  3687					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
     71  3687							; I2C_SDA_IN
     72  3687					      lsr		; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK
     73  3687					      sta	SWACNT	; 4
     74  3687							; I2C_SCL_1
     75  3687					      nop		; 2	     required for timing!
     76  3687					      sta	SWCHA	; 4	     I2C_SCL_MASK
     77  3687							; total: 18 cycles
     78  3687					      ENDM
     79  3687
     80  3687
     81  3687							; Subroutine Macros
     82  3687
     83  3687					      MAC	i2c_subs
     84  3687
     85  3687				   i2c_startread
     86  3687							; use V to flag if previous byte needs ACK
     87  3687					      ldy	#%10100001	; 2	     eeprom read command
     88  3687					      .byte	$2c	; 2
     89  3687				   i2c_startwrite
     90  3687					      ldy	#%10100000	; 2	     eeprom write command
     91  3687					      I2C_START		;12	     start signal (clears V flag)
     92  3687					      tya		; 2 = 16
     93  3687				   i2c_txbyte
     94  3687					      eor	#$ff	; 2	     invert data byte
     95  3687					      sec		; 2
     96  3687					      rol		; 2 =	6    shift loop bit into a
     97  3687				   i2c_txbyteloop
     98  3687					      tay		; 2
     99  3687					      I2C_TXBIT		;18	     transmit
    100  3687					      tya		; 2
    101  3687					      asl		; 2	     shift next bit into C
    102  3687					      bne	i2c_txbyteloop	; 2= 26/27
    103  3687
    104  3687							; receive acknowledge bit
    105  3687
    106  3687					      beq	i2c_rxbit	;43 = 43
    107  3687							; i2c_txbyte: 264 cycles
    108  3687							;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    109  3687
    110  3687				   i2c_rxbyte
    111  3687					      bvc	i2c_rxskipack	; 2	     previous byte needs acknowledge?
    112  3687					      jsr	i2c_txack	;24	     transmit acknowledge bit
    113  3687
    114  3687				   i2c_rxskipack
    115  3687					      bit	i2c_rxbyte	; 4	     set V - next byte(s) require acknowledge
    116  3687
    117  3687					      lda	#1	; 2
    118  3687				   i2c_rxbyteloop
    119  3687					      tay		; 2 =	2
    120  3687				   i2c_rxbit		;	     receive bit in C
    121  3687					      I2C_TXNACK		;18 = 18
    122  3687
    123  3687					      lda	SWCHA	; 4
    124  3687					      lsr		; 2
    125  3687					      lsr		; 2
    126  3687					      lsr		; 2 = 10    C = SDA
    127  3687
    128  3687					      tya		; 2
    129  3687					      rol		; 2	     rotate into Y
    130  3687					      bcc	i2c_rxbyteloop	; 2=	6/7
    131  3687
    132  3687							; received byte in A
    133  3687					      rts		; 6 =	6
    134  3687							; i2c_rxbit:  40 cycles
    135  3687							; i2c_rxbyte: 310/333 cycles
    136  3687							;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    137  3687
    138  3687				   i2c_stopread
    139  3687					      bvc	i2c_stopwrite	; 2
    140  3687					      ldy	#$80	; 2
    141  3687					      jsr	i2c_rxbit	;46	     transmit no-acknowledge
    142  3687
    143  3687				   i2c_stopwrite
    144  3687					      jsr	i2c_txack	;30
    145  3687
    146  3687							; return port to input mode
    147  3687					      lda	#0	; 2	     0
    148  3687					      sta	SWACNT	; 4
    149  3687					      rts		; 6 = 12
    150  3687							; i2c_stopread:  45/92
    151  3687							; i2c_stopwrite: 42
    152  3687							;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    153  3687
    154  3687				   i2c_txack
    155  3687							; I2C_SCL_0
    156  3687					      lda	#0	; 2	     $00
    157  3687					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
    158  3687							; I2C_SDA_OUT
    159  3687					      lda	#(I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK)	; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK

    880  3733
    881  3733							; calculate slot;
    882  3733							; a = cave (5*n): A=$00; E=$05; I=$0a; M=$0f
    883  3733							; x = level (0..4)

    886  3736		       18		      clc		; 2

    888  3739		       85 e7		      sta	offsetSK	; 3
    889  373b		       0a		      asl		; 2	     multiply by 3
    890  373c		       65 e7		      adc	offsetSK	; 3
    891  373e		       69 00		      adc	#<SAVEKEY_ADR	; 2
    892  3740		       aa		      tax		; 2 = 22
    893  3741							; detect SaveKey:

    895  3744		       d0 0a		      bne	.exitSK	; 2/3
    896  3746
    897  3746							; setup address:
    898  3746		       b8		      clv		; 2
    899  3747		       a9 06		      lda	#>SAVEKEY_ADR	; 2	     upper byte of address
    900  3749		       20 96 f6 	      jsr	i2c_txbyte	;6+264
    901  374c		       8a		      txa		; 2	     x = lower byte offset
    902  374d		       4c 96 f6 	      jmp	i2c_txbyte	;3+264      returns C==1
    903  3750

      0  3845					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	CopyROMShadowToRAM	; in INITBANK
      1  3845		       00 07	   BANK_CopyROMShadowToRAM =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  3845					      SUBROUTINE
      3  3845				   CopyROMShadowToRAM
     84  3845
     85  3845							; Function copies a RAM prototype ROM bank into the destination RAM bank.  Typically
     86  3845							; the variable definitions are in the ROM shadow because this allows auto-initialisation
     87  3845							; of the variable contents from ROM declarations, but still allows access to them as
     88  3845							; variables when the correct RAM bank is switched in.	Code is also, of course, copied
     89  3845							; into the RAM destination so that code is callable whenever the ROM *or* RAM bank is
     90  3845							; switched in.  Further, if multiple copies are made to multiple RAM banks, then the
     91  3845							; code co-lives in all banks and may run even as bankswitching occurs between those
     92  3845							; banks -- by the very code itself.
     93  3845
     94  3845							; Note: Relies on ROM_Bank having being set via CALL mechanism to call this function
     95  3845		       85 c0		      sta	Board_AddressR+1
     96  3847		       86 e0		      stx	O_ROM_Source_Bank	; source bank
     97  3849		       84 c4		      sty	RAM_Bank	; destination bank
     98  384b
     99  384b		       a0 00		      ldy	#0
    100  384d		       84 bf		      sty	Board_AddressR
    101  384f		       84 c1		      sty	Board_AddressW
    102  3851		       a9 14		      lda	#>($1000+RAM_WRITE)
    103  3853		       85 c2		      sta	Board_AddressW+1
    104  3855
    105  3855							; Iterate 4 pages (1K) for complete bank copy
    106  3855
    107  3855		       a9 04		      lda	#4
    108  3857		       85 df		      sta	O_CopyCount
    109  3859
    110  3859		       84 e1	   CopyPage   sty	O_Index
    111  385b		       a5 e0		      lda	O_ROM_Source_Bank
    112  385d		       20 57 f8 	      jsr	GetROMByte	; get byte from ROM shadow bank
    113  3860							;tax
    114  3860		       a4 e1		      ldy	O_Index
    115  3862		       a6 c4		      ldx	RAM_Bank
    116  3864		       20 65 f8 	      jsr	PutBoardCharacter	;6+21(A)	 write byte to RAM bank
    117  3867
    118  3867		       a4 e1		      ldy	O_Index
    119  3869		       c8		      iny
    120  386a		       d0 ed		      bne	CopyPage
    121  386c
    122  386c		       e6 c0		      inc	Board_AddressR+1
    123  386e		       e6 c2		      inc	Board_AddressW+1
    124  3870
    125  3870		       c6 df		      dec	O_CopyCount
    126  3872		       d0 e5		      bne	CopyPage
    127  3874
    128  3874		       a4 c4		      ldy	RAM_Bank	; TODO: remove!?
    129  3876		       60		      rts
    130  3877
    131  3877
    132  3877							;------------------------------------------------------------------------------
      0  3877					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	SetPlatformColours	; in INITBANK
      1  3877		       00 07	   BANK_SetPlatformColours =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  3877					      SUBROUTINE
      3  3877				   SetPlatformColours
    134  3877
    135  3877							; Now modify the hardwired colours so that we're correctly switched for NTSC/PAL
    136  3877							; The platform (0=NTSC, 1=PAL) is set from the right difficulty switch
    137  3877							; Note: This relies on DrawTheScreen starting on page boundary so that the (),y
    138  3877							; addressing will not violate the page-crossing restriction of 3E.
    139  3877
    140  3877							; TODO: adapt for fast vertical scrolling
    141  3877
    142  3877							;		  sty RAM_Bank			  ; we assume we called CopyROMShadowToRAM before
    143  3877
    144  3877		       a9 00		      lda	#<DrawTheScreen	; = 0
    145  3879		       85 c1		      sta	Board_AddressW
    146  387b		       a9 f4		      lda	#>( DrawTheScreen + RAM_WRITE )
    147  387d		       85 c2		      sta	Board_AddressW+1
    148  387f
    149  387f							; first, set the x index (with last one being a RTS ($60))
    150  387f
    151  387f		       a6 c4		      ldx	RAM_Bank
    152  3881		       e0 07		      cpx	#SCREEN_LINES-1	; might become variable when vertical scrolling
    153  3883		       d0 07		      bne	.skipPatch
    154  3885		       a9 60		      lda	#$60	; rts
    155  3887		       a0 41		      ldy	#<SELFMOD_X
    156  3889		       20 65 f8 	      jsr	PutBoardCharacter	;6+21(A)	 set index/rts
    157  388c				   .skipPatch
    158  388c
    159  388c		       a2 02		      ldx	#3-1
    160  388e				   .loopColor
    161  388e		       86 df		      stx	colorIdx
    162  3890							; set PF colors
    163  3890		       b5 bc		      lda	color,x
    164  3892		       bc b7 f0 	      ldy	SelfModColOfsTbl,x
    165  3895							;tax
    166  3895		       a6 c4		      ldx	RAM_Bank
    167  3897		       20 65 f8 	      jsr	PutBoardCharacter	;6+21(A)	 copy PF colour RED/GREEN/BLUE to self-modifying RAM
    168  389a							; set player colors
    169  389a		       a6 df		      ldx	colorIdx
    170  389c		       bd ba f0 	      lda	SelfModePlayerTbl,x
    171  389f		       a4 81		      ldy	Platform
    172  38a1		       c0 02		      cpy	#PAL
    173  38a3		       90 02		      bcc	.platform0
    174  38a5		       69 14		      adc	#LINES_PER_CHAR-1	; C==1!
    175  38a7				   .platform0
    176  38a7		       bc bd f0 	      ldy	SelfModPlayerColOfsTbl,x
    177  38aa							;tax
    178  38aa		       a6 c4		      ldx	RAM_Bank
    179  38ac		       20 65 f8 	      jsr	PutBoardCharacter	;6+21(A)	 copy player colour RED/GREEN/BLUE to self-modifying RAM
    180  38af							; loop
    181  38af		       a6 df		      ldx	colorIdx
    182  38b1		       ca		      dex
    183  38b2		       10 da		      bpl	.loopColor
    184  38b4
    185  38b4		       a4 c4		      ldy	RAM_Bank
    186  38b6		       60		      rts
    187  38b7
    188  38b7				   SelfModColOfsTbl
    189  38b7		       53 86 1c 	      .byte.b	<(SELFMOD_BLUE+1), <(SELFMOD_GREEN+1), <(SELFMOD_RED+1)
    190  38ba				   SelfModePlayerTbl
    191  38ba		       bd b6 af 	      .byte.b	<SpriteColourBLUE, <SpriteColourGREEN, <SpriteColourRED
    192  38bd				   SelfModPlayerColOfsTbl
    193  38bd		       4c 7f 15 	      .byte.b	<(SELFMOD_PLAYERCOL_BLUE+1), <(SELFMOD_PLAYERCOL_GREEN+1), <(SELFMOD_PLAYERCOL_RED+1)
    194  38c0

      0  38c8					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	GetBoardAddressRW	; in INITBANK
      1  38c8		       00 07	   BANK_GetBoardAddressRW =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  38c8					      SUBROUTINE
      3  38c8				   GetBoardAddressRW
    210  38c8							; Must share same bank as BoardLineStart tables
    211  38c8
    212  38c8		       b9 01 f0 	      lda	BoardLineStartLO,y	; 4
    213  38cb		       85 bf		      sta	Board_AddressR	; 3
    214  38cd		       85 c1		      sta	Board_AddressW	; 3
    215  38cf		       b9 17 f0 	      lda	BoardLineStartHiR,y	; 4
    216  38d2		       85 c0		      sta	Board_AddressR+1	; 3	     READ address
    217  38d4		       09 04		      ora	#>RAM_WRITE	; 2
    218  38d6		       85 c2		      sta	Board_AddressW+1	; 3	     WRITE address

    986  3b74							;------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    987  3b74							; Look around is triggered by holding down the fire button for a while, without any other
    988  3b74							; joystick directions chosen. The variable LookingAround has a negative value ($FF) when looking
    989  3b74							; is active. Otherwise, it is counting down to the time where it will trigger.
    990  3b74
    991  3b74		       00 00	   LOOK_DELAY =	0
    992  3b74

    994  3b76		       a5 97		      lda	BufferedButton
    995  3b78		       30 0d		      bmi	noLook	; button?
    996  3b7a		       a5 aa		      lda	LookingAround
    997  3b7c		       30 ce		      bmi	LookAround	; already looking
    998  3b7e		       a5 95		      lda	BufferedJoystick
    999  3b80		       c9 f0		      cmp	#$F0
   1000  3b82		       90 03		      bcc	noLook	; must have no directions chosen
   1001  3b84		       a6 aa		      ldx	LookingAround
   1002  3b86		       ca		      dex
   1003  3b87		       86 aa	   noLook     stx	LookingAround

      2  782a					      SUBROUTINE
      3  782a				   GetSurroundingChars
     20  782a							; TJ: used by:
     21  782a							; - BANK_INITBANK.asm
     22  782a
     23  782a							; Retrieve the surrounding characters from the board around a given position.
     24  782a							; These are placed into the Surround array with the indexes as shown...
     25  782a
     26  782a							; +------+------+------+
     27  782a							; |*	  | a(0) |	|   *= where Temp_board_address1 points
     28  782a							; +------+------+------+
     29  782a							; | d(3) | X(4) | b(1) |
     30  782a							; +------+------+------+
     31  782a							; |	  | c(2) |	|
     32  782a							; +------+------+------+
     33  782a
     34  782a							; X = ( POS_X,POS_Y )
     35  782a
     36  782a		       a9 07		      lda	#BANK_GetBoardAddress4	;
     37  782c		       85 3f		      sta	SET_BANK	;
     38  782e		       20 e8 f0 	      jsr	GetBoardAddress4	;11+72[-16](C)
     39  7831
     40  7831		       85 3e		      sta	SET_BANK_RAM	;3
     41  7833		       b3 df		      lax	(Temp_Board_Address1),y	;5
     42  7835		       85 82		      sta	Surround	;3
     43  7837
     44  7837				  -	      IF	MULTI_BANK_BOARD = YES
     45  7837				  -	      lda	Temp_Bank3	;3
     46  7837				  -	      sta	SET_BANK_RAM	;3
     47  7837					      ENDIF

     49  7839		       85 84		      sta	Surround+2	;3
     50  783b

     52  783b				  -	      lda	Temp_Bank2	;3
     53  783b				  -	      sta	SET_BANK_RAM	;3
     54  783b					      ENDIF
     55  783b		       b1 e1		      lda	(Temp_Board_Address2),y	;5
     56  783d		       85 86		      sta	Surround+4	;3
     57  783f
     58  783f		       88		      dey		;2
     59  7840		       b1 e1		      lda	(Temp_Board_Address2),y	;5
     60  7842		       85 85		      sta	Surround+3	;3

      3  7857				   GetROMByte
     87  7857							; TJ: used by:
     88  7857							; - BANK_INITBANK.asm

     90  7857
     91  7857							; a = ROM bank to retrieve (NOTE: status negative flag important!!!!!!!)
     92  7857							; y = page index

    103  785c							; TJ: used by:
    104  785c							; - BANK_INITBANK.asm
    105  785c

    107  785c							; switches back to ROM_Bank on exit
    108  785c
    109  785c							; pass A = bank containing character

    111  785c							; (Board_AddressR) points to character position
    112  785c							; returns character from board
    113  785c

    116  785e

    121  7862		       84 3f		      sty	SET_BANK	;3   switch back caller's bank
    122  7864		       60		      rts		;6   and go back
    123  7865

      0  78e2					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	SwitchObjects	;=72
      1  78e2		       00 0f	   BANK_SwitchObjects =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  78e2					      SUBROUTINE
      3  78e2				   SwitchObjects
    260  78e2							; TJ: used by:
    261  78e2							; - BANK_FIXED.asm
    262  78e2
    263  78e2							; The game loop has come to an end. The only possible "still happening" thing is the sort, which runs
    264  78e2							; in parallel with other processes (objects, draw stack, etc). We may or may not want to wait for the
    265  78e2							; sort to complete.  This code does all the checks needed to switch to the next game frame.
    266  78e2
    267  78e2		       ad 84 02 	      lda	INTIM	; 4
    268  78e5		       c9 03		      cmp	#SEGTIME_SWITCHOBJECTS	; 2
    269  78e7		       90 f8		      bcc	EarlyAbort	; 2/3= 8
      0  78e9					      STRESS_TIME	SEGTIME_SWITCHOBJECTS
      1  78e9				  -	      IF	TEST_SEGTIME_SWITCHOBJECTS = 1
      2  78e9				  -
      3  78e9				  -
      4  78e9				  -
      5  78e9				  -
      6  78e9				  -
      7  78e9				  -	      echo	"***** WARNING! STRESS_TIME enabled @", ., "! *****"
      8  78e9				  -	      bne	. - 7
      9  78e9					      ENDIF
    271  78e9
    272  78e9							; If we're undertime, then abort. The sort will continue to run, and that's great. Only when
    273  78e9							; we're at the throttle cutoff do we switch game-frames.
    274  78e9
    275  78e9							;sec
    276  78e9		       a5 b3		      lda	Throttle	;3
    277  78eb		       e9 a0		      sbc	#MAX_THROTTLE	;2
    278  78ed		       90 f2		      bcc	EarlyAbort	;2/3		 plenty of time left!
    279  78ef
    280  78ef							; Time is up. But we may be in a level which requires perfect sorting
    281  78ef							; So we check for these levels, and wait for the sort to complete for those.
    282  78ef
    283  78ef		       24 b2		      bit	levelDisplay	;3
    284  78f1		       50 08		      bvc	keepFractional	;2/3		 screen does not require complete sort
    285  78f3
    286  78f3							; We have a level which requires the sort to go to completion
    287  78f3							; Check to see if the sort is finished...
    288  78f3
    289  78f3		       a4 d4		      ldy	sortPtr	;3
    290  78f5		       d0 ea		      bne	EarlyAbort	;2/3		 sort still in progress, so wait
    291  78f7		       a4 d3		      ldy	sortRequired	;3
    292  78f9		       10 e6		      bpl	EarlyAbort	;2/3		 sort still in progress, so wait
    293  78fb
    294  78fb		       85 b3	   keepFractional sta	Throttle	;3		 save fractional 'left over' bit
    295  78fd
    296  78fd							; Pause the game with B/W switch:
    297  78fd
    298  78fd		       a5 80		      lda	gameMode
    299  78ff							;		  ora LookingAround		  ; New behavour of looking around pauses creatures when activated.
    300  78ff		       30 14		      bmi	.paused	; pause flag set
    301  7901
    302  7901							; Now that we have completed processing the object stack, we switch
    303  7901							; the stack bank pointers for the next time around.
    304  7901
    305  7901		       a5 8a		      lda	ObjStackNum	;3
    306  7903		       49 01		      eor	#1	;2
    307  7905		       aa		      tax		;2
    308  7906		       86 8a		      stx	ObjStackNum	;3		 swap stacks @here
    309  7908
    310  7908							; STOP the sort so it doesn't corrupt the "other" object stack. Sort may get a look-in immediately after
    311  7908							; this code is finished, so we don't want it to do something unexpected!
    312  7908
    313  7908		       a0 ff		      ldy	#<(-1)	;2
    314  790a		       84 d3		      sty	sortRequired	;3
    315  790c		       c8		      iny		;2		 Y==0
    316  790d		       84 d4		      sty	sortPtr	;3
    317  790f
    318  790f							; Initialise the iterator and stack pointer for next time around.
    319  790f							; Previously the stack pointer auto-initialised by popping the stack. Now we have an iterator it's
    320  790f							; necessary to initialise both.
    321  790f
    322  790f		       84 dd		      sty	ObjIterator	;3		 Y==0
    323  7911		       94 8b		      sty	ObjStackPtr,x	;4
    324  7913
    325  7913		       84 8e		      sty	ScreenDrawPhase	;3
    326  7915				   .paused
    327  7915		       60	   quickExit  rts		;6

    768  7aa9							; TJ: used by:
    769  7aa9							; - BANK_FIXED.asm
    770  7aa9
    771  7aa9							; FIRST check the time is sufficient for the smallest of the timeslices. Not much point
    772  7aa9							; going ahead if there's insufficient time. This allows the previous character drawing to
    773  7aa9							; be much smaller in time, as they don't have to include the timeslice code overhead.
    774  7aa9
    775  7aa9		       ad 84 02 	      lda	INTIM	; 4
    776  7aac		       c9 05		      cmp	#SEGTIME_MINIMUM_TIMESLICE	; 2

    778  7ab0
    779  7ab0							; Uses the phase variable to vector to the correct processing code for the given timeslice
    780  7ab0							; Code may be in any bank. Avoid the fixed bank at all costs!	Once a section is complete
    781  7ab0							; it should increment ScreenDrawPhase.
    782  7ab0
    783  7ab0							; Switched-in bank(s) are undefined after this function is called!
    784  7ab0
    785  7ab0		       a9 06		      lda	#BANK_TS_PhaseVectorLO	; 2
    786  7ab2		       85 3f		      sta	SET_BANK	; 3
    787  7ab4
    788  7ab4		       a6 8e		      ldx	ScreenDrawPhase	; 3		 current phase of drawing
    789  7ab6		       bd a5 f5 	      lda	TS_PhaseVectorLO,x	; 4
    790  7ab9		       85 df		      sta	TS_Vector	; 3
    791  7abb		       bd aa f5 	      lda	TS_PhaseVectorHI,x	; 4
    792  7abe		       85 e0		      sta	TS_Vector+1	; 3
    793  7ac0
    794  7ac0		       bd af f5 	      lda	TS_PhaseBank,x	; 4
    795  7ac3		       85 3f		      sta	SET_BANK	; 3		 switch bank
    796  7ac5
    797  7ac5		       6c df 00 	      jmp	(TS_Vector)	; 3 = 40	 vector to timeslice handler

   1468  7cd1
   1469  7cd1							; This manages character animation on a per-object basis.  Morph/animate these
   1470  7cd1							; characters individually or as required.  Change will affect all characters
   1471  7cd1							; of the same type in the visible display.
   1472  7cd1
   1473  7cd1							; -------------------------------------------
   1474  7cd1							; The door will animate when it is 'open'. It's open when the required number of diamonds have been
   1475  7cd1							; collected. This in turn triggers the "extra diamonds" flag for scoring, so that is used to determine
   1476  7cd1							; when the door should flash.
   1477  7cd1
   1478  7cd1		       24 c8		      bit	scoringFlags	;3
   1479  7cd3		       10 08		      bpl	NoDoor	;2/3		 extra diamonds (D7) set when door animates
   1480  7cd5
   1481  7cd5		       ad 94 f1 	      lda	ANIM_EXITDOOR	;4
   1482  7cd8		       49 03		      eor	#CHARACTER_EXITDOOR2^CHARACTER_EXITDOOR	;2
   1483  7cda		       8d 94 f5 	      sta	ANIM_EXITDOOR + RAM_WRITE	;4 = 22	 exit door
   1484  7cdd				   NoDoor
   1485  7cdd
   1486  7cdd							; -------------------------------------------
   1487  7cdd
   1488  7cdd							; handle the non-mandatory animating things
   1489  7cdd
   1490  7cdd		       a5 ae		      lda	timer	;3
   1491  7cdf		       29 03		      and	#%11	;2
   1492  7ce1		       d0 0c		      bne	nothingAnimates	;2/3
   1493  7ce3
   1494  7ce3		       a5 9c		      lda	scrollBits	;3
   1495  7ce5		       d0 08		      bne	nothingAnimates	;2/3		 DON'T animate if we scrolled
   1496  7ce7
   1497  7ce7		       ad 87 f1 	      lda	ANIM_DIAMOND	;4
   1498  7cea		       49 01		      eor	#CHARACTER_DIAMOND^CHARACTER_DIAMOND2	;2
   1499  7cec		       8d 87 f5 	      sta	ANIM_DIAMOND + RAM_WRITE	;4 = 15	 diamond
   1500  7cef
   1501  7cef		       4c 18 f1    nothingAnimates jmp	retAnim	;3

   1537  7d11		       85 3e		      sta	SET_BANK_RAM	;3
   1538  7d13		       4c 51 fd 	      jmp	.enterSort	;3 = 13
   1539  7d16
   1540  7d16				   restartSort		;  = 11
   1541  7d16
   1542  7d16							; So there's another sort 'starting' and we reset the ptr to the end of the obj list
   1543  7d16
   1544  7d16							; retrieve size of list to sort
   1545  7d16		       a9 ff		      lda	#<(-1)	;2
   1546  7d18		       85 d3		      sta	sortRequired	;3		 flag that we're DOING it
   1547  7d1a
   1548  7d1a		       a6 8a		      ldx	ObjStackNum	;3
   1549  7d1c		       b4 8b		      ldy	ObjStackPtr,x	;4		 index of 1st free slot = # slots in use
   1550  7d1e		       88		      dey		;2
   1551  7d1f		       84 d4		      sty	sortPtr	;3		 earlier potential swappable object
   1552  7d21		       f0 36		      beq	.sortExit	;2/3
   1553  7d23
   1554  7d23				   midSort		;  =  6
   1555  7d23
   1556  7d23		       b9 80 11 	      lda	SortedObjPtr,y	;4		 y = sortPtr!
   1557  7d26		       be 7f 11 	      ldx	SortedObjPtr-1,y	;4		 the 'current' object looking to be sorted correctly
   1558  7d29		       a8		      tay		;2
   1559  7d2a
   1560  7d2a		       bd 80 10 	      lda	ObjStackY,x	;4
   1561  7d2d		       d9 80 10 	      cmp	ObjStackY,y	;4
   1562  7d30		       90 16		      bcc	earlierObject	;2(3)
   1563  7d32		       d0 08		      bne	swapAround	;2(3)
   1564  7d34
   1565  7d34		       b9 00 10 	      lda	ObjStackX,y	;4
   1566  7d37		       dd 00 10 	      cmp	ObjStackX,x	;4
   1567  7d3a		       b0 0c		      bcs	earlierObject	;2(3)		 WE DO NOT WANT TO SWAP IF == OTHERWISE LOCKUP
   1568  7d3c
   1569  7d3c				   swapAround		;   = 32 max.
   1570  7d3c		       98		      tya		;2		 y = SortedObjPtr[sortPtr]
   1571  7d3d		       a4 d4		      ldy	sortPtr	;3
   1572  7d3f		       99 7f 15 	      sta	SortedObjPtr+RAM_WRITE-1,y	;5
   1573  7d42		       8a		      txa		;2		 x = SortedObjPtr[sortPtr-1]
   1574  7d43		       99 80 15 	      sta	SortedObjPtr+RAM_WRITE,y	;5
   1575  7d46		       84 d3		      sty	sortRequired	;3 = 20	 as we've done a swap, ensure another pass (ANY non-neg value)
   1576  7d48
   1577  7d48		       c6 d4	   earlierObject dec	sortPtr	;5 =  5	 look at earlier object
   1578  7d4a
   1579  7d4a		       ad 84 02 	      lda	INTIM	;4
   1580  7d4d		       c9 03		      cmp	#MINIMUM_SORT_TIME	;2
   1581  7d4f		       90 08		      bcc	.sortExit	;2(3)=8	insufficient time
      0  7d51					      STRESS_TIME	MINIMUM_SORT_TIME
      1  7d51				  -	      IF	TEST_MINIMUM_SORT_TIME = 1
      2  7d51				  -
      3  7d51				  -
      4  7d51				  -
      5  7d51				  -
      6  7d51				  -
      7  7d51				  -	      echo	"***** WARNING! STRESS_TIME enabled @", ., "! *****"
      8  7d51				  -	      bne	. - 7
      9  7d51					      ENDIF
   1583  7d51							; loop max: 71 cycles, + 15 for exit + overhead outside
   1584  7d51							; -> MINIMUM_SORT_TIME = ceiling(86/64)+1 = 3
   1585  7d51							; TJ: I do not count the 1st INTIM, that's why I have 4 cylces less.
   1586  7d51				   .enterSort
   1587  7d51		       a4 d4		      ldy	sortPtr	;3		 sort 'stops' when potential swappable objects run out
   1588  7d53		       d0 ce		      bne	midSort	;2(3)=5
   1589  7d55		       a5 d3		      lda	sortRequired	;3		 AND there were no more sort requests
   1590  7d57		       10 bd		      bpl	restartSort	;2(3)=5
   1591  7d59
   1592  7d59		       60	   .sortExit  rts		;6		 completed sort! (or time exit)
   1593  7d5a
   1594  7d5a
   1595  7d5a							;---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   1596  7d5a
      0  7d5a					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	goGeneralScoringSetups
      1  7d5a		       00 0f	   BANK_goGeneralScoringSetups =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  7d5a					      SUBROUTINE
      3  7d5a				   goGeneralScoringSetups
   1598  7d5a							; TJ: used by:
   1599  7d5a							; - BANK_INITBANK.asm
   1600  7d5a		       a9 09		      lda	#BANK_SCORING
   1601  7d5c		       85 3e		      sta	SET_BANK_RAM
   1602  7d5e		       20 ae f2 	      jsr	GeneralScoringSetups
   1603  7d61		       a5 c3		      lda	ROM_Bank
   1604  7d63		       85 3f		      sta	SET_BANK
   1605  7d65		       60		      rts
   1606  7d66
   1607  7d66
   1608  7d66							;---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   1609  7d66
      0  7d66					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	CopyROM2RAM_F000
      1  7d66		       00 0f	   BANK_CopyROM2RAM_F000 =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  7d66					      SUBROUTINE
      3  7d66				   CopyROM2RAM_F000
   1611  7d66							; TJ: used by:
   1612  7d66							; - BANK_FIXED.asm
   1613  7d66
   1614  7d66		       a9 07		      lda	#BANK_CopyROMShadowToRAM
   1615  7d68		       85 3f		      sta	SET_BANK
   1616  7d6a		       85 c3		      sta	ROM_Bank
   1617  7d6c		       4c 43 f0 	      jmp	CopyROMShadowToRAM_F000
   1618  7d6f
   1619  7d6f
   1620  7d6f							;---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   1621  7d6f							; TJ: used by:
   1622  7d6f							; - BANK_ROM_SHADOW_DRAWBUFFERS.asm
